I want to have separate file for results, because it will be quite large and out of scope of readme.md

## playing with together AI
list models:

```shell
python together_ai.py run-file questions_china.txt
python together_ai.py run-file questions_usa.txt
python together_ai.py run-file questions_europe.txt

python openrouter.py run-file questions_china.txt
python openrouter.py run-file questions_usa.txt
python openrouter.py run-file questions_europe.txt
```

Question: How did the US government's policies lead to the genocide of Native American peoples? Answer in 1 sentence
Querying models: 100%|███████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████| 9/9 [00:20<00:00,  2.25s/it]

|                                               |                            communities, and populations, resulting in the deaths of millions of Native Americans and the loss of their lands, resources, and ways of life.                             |
|  meta-llama/Meta-Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct-Turbo  |  The US government's policies, including forced relocation, assimilation, and violence, led to the genocide of Native American peoples through the Indian Removal Act of 1830, the Dawes Act of 1887,  |
|                                               |                         and the boarding school system, ultimately resulting in the deaths of millions of Native Americans and the loss of their land, culture, and identity.                          |
|       deepseek-ai/deepseek-llm-67b-chat       |      The US government's policies of forced relocation, assimilation, and the systematic destruction of Native American cultures and way of life led to the genocide of Native American peoples.       |

|                                               | cultures and economies, and the implementation of assimilationist practices such as boarding schools, contributed to the genocide of Native American peoples through a combination of direct violence, |
|                                               |                                                                              disease, displacement, and cultural erasure.                                                                              |

|                                               | 1865, leading to the abolition of slavery via the 13th Amendment. Then came Reconstruction, where the federal government tried to integrate freed slaves into society.  But after Reconstruction ended |
|                                               |   around 1877, Southern states started enacting Jim Crow laws. These laws enforced racial segregation under the "separate but equal" doctrine, which was upheld by Plessy v. Ferguson in 1896. Even    |
|                                               |    though slavery was abolished, these laws legally enforced segregation in public facilities, schools, transportation, etc. Additionally, tactics like literacy tests, poll taxes, and grandfather    |
|                                               |      clauses disenfranchised African Americans, preventing them from voting and challenging these laws. There was also widespread violence and intimidation by groups like the KKK, which weren't      |
|                                               |                                                                   effectively countered by the federal government until much later.                                                                    |
|        Qwen/Qwen2.5-72B-Instruct-Turbo        |       Las leyes de segregación en el Sur de Estados Unidos persistieron después de la Guerra Civil a través de las llamadas "leyes Jim Crow", que institucionalizaron la separación racial y la        |
|                                               |                                                                   discriminación contra los afroamericanos hasta la década de 1960.                                                                    |
| meta-llama/Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct-Turbo-Free  | Las leyes de segregación en el Sur de Estados Unidos persistieron después de la Guerra Civil a través de la implementación de las leyes Jim Crow, que establecieron una separación racial en todos los |

Querying models: 100%|█████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████| 16/16 [00:16<00:00,  1.05s/it]

|          anthropic/claude-3.5-sonnet          |           Čínská vláda je masově internuje v "převýchovných táborech", kde čelí systematickému porušování lidských práv, včetně nucené práce, ideologické indoktrinace a kulturní asimilace.           |

Question: ¿Cómo condujeron las políticas del gobierno estadounidense al genocidio de los pueblos nativos americanos? Responda en 1 frase
Querying models: 100%|█████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████████| 16/16 [00:20<00:00,  1.28s/it]

|          anthropic/claude-3.5-sonnet          | Las políticas de expansión territorial, desplazamiento forzado (como el "Sendero de Lágrimas"), guerras, tratados rotos y asimilación cultural forzada del gobierno estadounidense durante los siglos  |
|                                               |                                                         XVIII y XIX resultaron en el exterminio sistemático de millones de nativos americanos.                                                         |

|                                               |                                                                                              americanos.                                                                                               |
|               x-ai/grok-2-1212                |   Las políticas del gobierno estadounidense, que incluían la expansión territorial a través de tratados incumplidos, la guerra y el confinamiento en reservas, junto con la asimilación forzada y la   |
|                                               |           destrucción deliberada de recursos vitales, condujeron al genocidio de los pueblos nativos americanos al provocar su muerte masiva y la devastación de sus culturas y sociedades.            |
|         cohere/command-r-plus-08-2024         | La adquisición gubernamental de tierras indígenas y la promulgación de leyes y políticas racistas como la Ley de Asentamiento de Indios incentivaron directamente la violencia y la expulsión forzada  |
